\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l01496}01496\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ out[pos]\ =\ (np.power(x[pos]\ +\ 1,\ lmbda)\ -\/\ 1)\ /\ lmbda}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l01498}01498\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ when\ x\ <\ 0}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02395}02395\ \ \ \ \ Zstar\ =\ np.unique(Z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02396}02396\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ Zstar.size\ <\ 2:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02397}02397\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{raise}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classValueError}{ValueError}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}anderson\_ksamp\ needs\ more\ than\ one\ distinct\ "{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02398}02398\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}observation"{}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02399}02399\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02400}02400\ \ \ \ \ n\ =\ np.array([sample.size\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ sample\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{in}\ samples])}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02405}02405\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ midrank:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02406}02406\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A2kN\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescipy_1_1stats_1_1__morestats_a9b8bfd0f7f8a99f24676999a1d6a1081}{\_anderson\_ksamp\_midrank}}(samples,\ Z,\ Zstar,\ k,\ n,\ N)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02409}02409\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02410}02410\ \ \ \ \ H\ =\ (1.\ /\ n).sum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02411}02411\ \ \ \ \ hs\_cs\ =\ (1.\ /\ arange(N\ -\/\ 1,\ 1,\ -\/1)).cumsum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02412}02412\ \ \ \ \ h\ =\ hs\_cs[-\/1]\ +\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02413}02413\ \ \ \ \ g\ =\ (hs\_cs\ /\ arange(2,\ N)).sum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02414}02414\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02415}02415\ \ \ \ \ a\ =\ (4*g\ -\/\ 6)\ *\ (k\ -\/\ 1)\ +\ (10\ -\/\ 6*g)*H}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02416}02416\ \ \ \ \ b\ =\ (2*g\ -\/\ 4)*k**2\ +\ 8*h*k\ +\ (2*g\ -\/\ 14*h\ -\/\ 4)*H\ -\/\ 8*h\ +\ 4*g\ -\/\ 6}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02417}02417\ \ \ \ \ c\ =\ (6*h\ +\ 2*g\ -\/\ 2)*k**2\ +\ (4*h\ -\/\ 4*g\ +\ 6)*k\ +\ (2*h\ -\/\ 6)*H\ +\ 4*h}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02418}02418\ \ \ \ \ d\ =\ (2*h\ +\ 6)*k**2\ -\/\ 4*h*k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02419}02419\ \ \ \ \ sigmasq\ =\ (a*N**3\ +\ b*N**2\ +\ c*N\ +\ d)\ /\ ((N\ -\/\ 1.)\ *\ (N\ -\/\ 2.)\ *\ (N\ -\/\ 3.))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02420}02420\ \ \ \ \ m\ =\ k\ -\/\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02421}02421\ \ \ \ \ A2\ =\ (A2kN\ -\/\ m)\ /\ math.sqrt(sigmasq)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02422}02422\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02423}02423\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ The\ b\_i\ values\ are\ the\ interpolation\ coefficients\ from\ Table\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02424}02424\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ of\ Scholz\ and\ Stephens\ 1987}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02425}02425\ \ \ \ \ b0\ =\ np.array([0.675,\ 1.281,\ 1.645,\ 1.96,\ 2.326,\ 2.573,\ 3.085])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02426}02426\ \ \ \ \ b1\ =\ np.array([-\/0.245,\ 0.25,\ 0.678,\ 1.149,\ 1.822,\ 2.364,\ 3.615])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02427}02427\ \ \ \ \ b2\ =\ np.array([-\/0.105,\ -\/0.305,\ -\/0.362,\ -\/0.391,\ -\/0.396,\ -\/0.345,\ -\/0.154])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02428}02428\ \ \ \ \ critical\ =\ b0\ +\ b1\ /\ math.sqrt(m)\ +\ b2\ /\ m}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02429}02429\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02430}02430\ \ \ \ \ sig\ =\ np.array([0.25,\ 0.1,\ 0.05,\ 0.025,\ 0.01,\ 0.005,\ 0.001])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02431}02431\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ A2\ <\ critical.min():}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02432}02432\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ p\ =\ sig.max()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02433}02433\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ warnings.warn(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}p-\/value\ capped:\ true\ value\ larger\ than\ \{\}"{}}.format(p),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02434}02434\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ stacklevel=2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02435}02435\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif}\ A2\ >\ critical.max():}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02436}02436\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ p\ =\ sig.min()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02437}02437\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ warnings.warn(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}p-\/value\ floored:\ true\ value\ smaller\ than\ \{\}"{}}.format(p),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02438}02438\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ stacklevel=2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02439}02439\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02440}02440\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ interpolation\ of\ probit\ of\ significance\ level}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l02660}02660\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:\ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ N\ even}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04144}04144\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ correction:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04145}04145\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ alternative\ ==\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}two-\/sided"{}}:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04155}04155\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ prob\ =\ 2.\ *\ distributions.norm.sf(abs(z))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04156}04156\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif}\ alternative\ ==\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}greater"{}}:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04169}04169\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ r\_plus\ is\ the\ center\ of\ the\ distribution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04170}04170\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ prob\ =\ 1.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04171}04171\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04172}04172\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ p\_less\ =\ np.sum(pmf[:r\_plus\ +\ 1])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04173}04173\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ p\_greater\ =\ np.sum(pmf[r\_plus:])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04174}04174\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ prob\ =\ 2*min(p\_greater,\ p\_less)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04177}04177\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04178}04178\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ prob\ =\ np.sum(pmf[:r\_plus\ +\ 1])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__morestats_8py_source_l04179}04179\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ prob\ =\ np.clip(prob,\ 0,\ 1)}
